### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: Resource and Collection URL Formats

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Defines the standard URL structures for accessing individual Resources and groups of Resources (Collections) within the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API. It also illustrates common filtering patterns for Collections, allowing users to narrow down results by specific keys or other criteria like login status.

```APIDOC
API Endpoints:

Resource Request Format:
  URL: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/{resource}/{resource_key}
  Description: Used to retrieve data for a single identifiable resource.
  Parameters:
    {resource}: The type of resource (e.g., 'league', 'player').
    {resource_key}: The unique identifier for the specific resource.

Collection Request Format:
  URL: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/{collection};{resource}_keys={resource_key1},{resource_key2}
  Description: Used to retrieve data for multiple similar resources, wrapped in a collection.
  Parameters:
    {collection}: The type of collection (e.g., 'leagues', 'players').
    {resource}_keys: Comma-separated list of unique identifiers for resources within the collection.

Collection Filtering Examples:
  Filter by specific player keys:
    URL: /fantasy/v2/;player_keys=,{player_key2}
    Description: Retrieves data for specified players within the players collection.

  Filter by logged-in user:
    URL: /fantasy/v2/;use_login=1
    Description: Retrieves data relevant to the currently logged-in user within a collection that supports this filter.
```

--------------------------------

### Leagues Collection API Reference

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Documentation for the Leagues API, enabling simultaneous retrieval of information from multiple leagues. Each element returned is a League Resource. It details supported HTTP operations and various URI formats for accessing league data and sub-resources.

```APIDOC
Leagues collection:
  Description: With the Leagues API, you can obtain information from a collection of leagues simultaneously. Each element beneath the Leagues Collection will be a League Resource.
  HTTP Operations Supported:
    - GET
  URIs:
    Any sub-resource valid for a league is a valid sub-resource under the leagues collection.
    Any sub-resource for a collection of leagues is extracted using a URI like:
      /leagues/{sub_resource}
    OR
      /leagues;league_keys={league_key1},{league_key2}/{sub_resource}
    Multiple sub-resources can be extracted from leagues in the same URI using a format like:
      /leagues;out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
    OR
      /leagues;league_keys={league_key1},{league_key2};out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
```

--------------------------------

### Define Yahoo Fantasy Sports Game API URI Structures

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Outlines the various URI structures for the Yahoo Fantasy Sports Game API, including the base endpoint, accessing sub-resources, and retrieving multiple sub-resources in a single request.

```APIDOC
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/game/
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/game//
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/game/;out=,{sub_resource_2}
```

--------------------------------

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: League Resource URIs

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Details the base URI for the League API and patterns for accessing sub-resources within a league, including how to extract multiple sub-resources in a single URI.

```APIDOC
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/league/

Any sub-resource under a league is extracted using a URI like:
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/league//

Multiple sub-resources can be extracted from league in the same URI using a format like:
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/league/;out=,{sub_resource_2}
```

### Query Yahoo Fantasy Sports Game Data with YQL

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Demonstrates how to retrieve fantasy game information using a YQL (Yahoo Query Language) SELECT statement, specifying the `game_key` to filter results.

```YQL
select * from fantasysports.games where game_key='nfl';
```

### Retrieve Game Information using YQL

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

This YQL query demonstrates how to fetch game information from the `fantasysports.games` table. It uses a `game_key` to specify the desired game, in this case, 'nfl', to retrieve details for the NFL fantasy game.

```YQL
select * from fantasysports.games where game_key='nfl';
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports Games Collection API Reference

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

This section describes the Games Collection API, which allows simultaneous retrieval of information for multiple games. Each element within the collection corresponds to a Game Resource, providing a consolidated view of various fantasy games.

```APIDOC
Games Collection API:
  Description: Obtain information from a collection of games simultaneously. Each element beneath the Games Collection will be a Game Resource.
  HTTP Operations Supported: GET
```

### Understand Yahoo Fantasy Sports Game Key Parameter Format

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Explains the valid formats for the `game_key` parameter in the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API, which can be either a `game_code` (e.g., 'pnfl') or a `game_id` (e.g., '223'). It also clarifies that `game_code`s are internally translated to `game_id`s.

```APIDOC
{game_code} or {game_id}
Example: pnfl or 223
```

--------------------------------

### Transactions Collection URI Formats

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Illustrates various URI formats for accessing sub-resources and extracting multiple sub-resources from the transactions collection, including options for specifying multiple transaction keys.

```APIDOC
Sub-resource URI: /transactions/{sub_resource}

Multiple transaction keys:
/transactions;transaction_keys={transaction_key1},{transaction_key2}/{sub_resource}

Multiple sub-resources:
/transactions;out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}

Multiple keys and sub-resources:
/transactions;transaction_keys={transaction_key1},{transaction_key2};out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
```

--------------------------------

### Transactions Collection URI Formats

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Explains various URI formats for accessing sub-resources under the transactions collection. This includes extracting single sub-resources, using multiple transaction keys, extracting multiple sub-resources, and combining transaction keys with multiple sub-resources.

```APIDOC
Transactions Collection URIs:
  - Single sub-resource: /transactions/{sub_resource}
  - Multiple transaction keys: /transactions;transaction_keys={transaction_key1},{transaction_key2}/{sub_resource}
  - Multiple sub-resources: /transactions;out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
  - Multiple transaction keys and sub-resources: /transactions;transaction_keys={transaction_key1},{transaction_key2};out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
```

--------------------------------

### Yahoo Fantasy API Resource Request Format

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Defines the URL structure for requesting a single resource from the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API. Resources typically describe chunks of data that can be identified by a unique key, allowing direct access to specific data entities. This format is used when retrieving information about a singular item like a specific league or game.

```APIDOC
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/{resource}/{resource_key}
```

--------------------------------

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: League Resource Overview

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Provides a general description of the League API within Yahoo Fantasy Sports. It explains that the API allows retrieval of league-related information such as league name, number of teams, and draft status. Leagues exist in the context of a particular game, and users can only retrieve data for private leagues they are members of, or for public leagues.

```APIDOC
When users join a Fantasy Football, Baseball, Basketball, or Hockey draft and trade game, they are organized into leagues with a limited number of friends or other Yahoo! users, with each user managing a Team. With the League API, you can obtain the league related information, like the league name, the number of teams, the draft status, et cetera. Leagues only exist in the context of a particular Game, although you can request a League Resource as the base of your URI by using the global. A particular user can only retrieve data for private leagues of which they are a member, or for public leagues.
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports Transaction API Endpoints

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Defines the base URI for the Yahoo Fantasy Sports Transaction API and illustrates how to construct URIs for accessing transaction data. It shows patterns for retrieving a single transaction, extracting specific sub-resources, and requesting multiple sub-resources within a single API call.

```APIDOC
Base URI: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/transaction/

Sub-resource URI: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/transaction//

Multiple Sub-resources URI: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/transaction/;out=,{sub_resource_2}
```

### Allow an Accepted Trade (PUT XML)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

For league commissioners, this XML snippet shows how to approve an accepted trade that is awaiting processing. The `action` element is set to 'allow' for the specified `transaction_key`.

```XML
<?xml version='1.0'?>
<fantasy_content>
  <transaction>
    <transaction_key>248.l.55438.pt.11</transaction_key>
    <type>pending_trade</type>
    <action>allow</action>
  </transaction>
</fantasy_content>
```

--------------------------------

### Yahoo Fantasy API Collection Request Format

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Defines the URL structure for requesting a collection of resources from the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API. Collections are wrappers that contain similar resources, allowing retrieval of multiple items by providing a comma-separated list of resource keys. This format is useful for fetching data across several related entities simultaneously.

```APIDOC
https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/{collection};{resource}_keys={resource_key1},{resource_key2}
```

```XML
              <percentage>.692</percentage>
            </outcome_totals>
            <divisional_outcome_totals>
              <wins>5</wins>
              <losses>1</losses>
              <ties>0</ties>
            </divisional_outcome_totals>
          </team_standings>
        </team>
        <team>
          <team_key>223.l.431.t.5</team_key>
          <team_id>5</team_id>
          <name>RotoExperts</name>
          <url>https://football.fantasysports.yahoo.com/archive/pnfl/2009/431/5</url>
          <team_logos>
```

### PHP OAuth Client for Yahoo Fantasy Sports API

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

This PHP script demonstrates a complete OAuth 1.0a flow for interacting with the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API. It handles storing and refreshing access tokens, facilitating user authentication, and making authenticated API requests. It requires the PHP OAuth extension and user-specific consumer key and secret.

```php
<?php
// **** POTENTIAL CONFIGURATION STARTS HERE ****

// NOTE: If you don't have the OAuth extension hooked into PHP, you may need
//  to include it here.

// MODIFY: Insert whichever URL you'd like to try below. By default, the
//  following URL will try to pull out the NFL teams for the logged-in user
$url = 'https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/users;use_login=1/games;game_keys=nfl/teams';
$scope = 'test';

// MODIFY: Insert your own consumer key and secret here!
$consumer_data = array();
$consumer_data['test']['key'] = '<INSERT CONSUMER KEY HERE>';
$consumer_data['test']['secret'] = '<INSERT CONSUMER SECRET HERE>';

// **** MAIN PROGRAM START HERE ****

$consumer_key = $consumer_data[$scope]['key'];
$consumer_secret = $consumer_data[$scope]['secret'];

// By default, try to store token information in /tmp folder
$token_file_name = '/tmp/oauth_data_token_storage_' . $consumer_key . '.out';

$access_token = NULL;
$access_secret = NULL;
$access_session = NULL;
$access_verifier = NULL;
$store_access_token_data = false;

if( file_exists( $token_file_name ) &&
    $tok_fh = fopen( $token_file_name, 'r' ) ) {

  $invalid_file = false;

  // Get first line: access token
  $access_token = fgets( $tok_fh );
  if( $access_token ) {
    // Get next line: access secret
    $access_secret = fgets( $tok_fh );
    if( $access_secret ) {
      // Get next line: access session handle
      $access_session = fgets( $tok_fh );
      if( ! $access_session ) {
        $invalid_file = true;
      }
    } else {
      $invalid_file = true;
    }
  } else {
    $invalid_file = true;
  }

  if( $invalid_file ) {
    print "File did not seem to be formatted correctly -- needs 3 lines with access token, secret, and session handle.\n";
    $access_token = NULL;
    $access_secret = NULL;
    $access_session = NULL;
  } else {
    print "Got access token information!\n";

    $access_token = rtrim( $access_token );
    $access_secret = rtrim( $access_secret );
    $access_session = rtrim( $access_session );

    print " Token: ${access_token}\n";
    print " Secret: ${access_secret}\n";
    print " Session Handle: ${access_session}\n\n";
  }

  // Done with file, close it up
  fclose( $tok_fh );

} else {
  print "Couldn't open ${token_file_name}, assuming we need to get a new request token.\n";
}

// 1. See if we have a stored access token/secret/session. If so, try to use
//    that token.
if( $access_token ) {

  $o = new OAuth( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret,
                  OAUTH_SIG_METHOD_HMACSHA1, OAUTH_AUTH_TYPE_URI );
  $o->enableDebug();

  $auth_failure = false;

  // Try to make request using stored token
  try {
    $o->setToken( $access_token, $access_secret );
    if( $o->fetch( $url ) ) {
      print "Got data from API:\n\n";
      print $o->getLastResponse() . "\n\n";

      print "Successful!\n";
      exit;
    } else {
      print "Couldn't fetch\n";
    }
  } catch( OAuthException $e ) {
    print 'Error: ' . $e->getMessage() . "\n";
    print 'Error Code: ' . $e->getCode() . "\n";
    print 'Response: ' . $e->lastResponse . "\n";

    if( $e->getCode() == 401 ) {
      $auth_failure = true;
    }
  }

  // 2. If we get an auth error, try to refresh the token using the session.
  if( $auth_failure ) {

    try {
      $response = $o->getAccessToken( 'https://api.login.yahoo.com/oauth/v2/get_token', $access_session, $access_verifier );
    } catch( OAuthException $e ) {
      print 'Error: ' . $e->getMessage() . "\n";
      print 'Response: ' . $e->lastResponse . "\n";

      $response = NULL;
    }

    print_r( $response );

    if( $response ) {
      $access_token = $response['oauth_token'];
      $access_secret = $response['oauth_token_secret'];
      $access_session = $response['oauth_session_handle'];
      $store_access_token_data = true;

      print "Was able to refresh access token:\n";
      print " Token: ${access_token}\n";
      print " Secret: ${access_secret}\n";
      print " Session Handle: ${access_session}\n\n";

    } else {

      $access_token = NULL;
      $access_secret = NULL;
      $access_session = NULL;
      print "Unable to refresh access token, will need to request a new one.\n";
    }
  }
}
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: Games Collection URIs

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Defines the URI patterns for accessing sub-resources within the games collection. This includes retrieving a single sub-resource, multiple sub-resources using game keys, and extracting multiple sub-resources from games in a single URI.

```APIDOC
/games/{sub_resource}
OR
/games;game_keys={game_key1},{game_key2}/{sub_resource}

Multiple sub-resources:
/games;out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
OR
/games;game_keys={game_key1},{game_key2};out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
```

--------------------------------

### Team Resource API Reference

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Documentation for the Team API, allowing retrieval of information about a specific team within Yahoo Fantasy Sports. This includes team name, managers, logos, stats, points, and rosters. Teams exist within the context of a League, and access is restricted to members of private leagues or public leagues.

```APIDOC
Team resource:
  Description: The Team APIs allow you to retrieve information about a team within our fantasy games. The team is the basic unit for keeping track of a roster of players, and can be managed by either one or two managers (the second manager being called a co-manager). With the Team APIs, you can obtain team-related information, like the team name, managers, logos, stats and points, and rosters for particular weeks. Teams only exist in the context of a particular League, although you can request a Team Resource as the base of your URI by using the global. A particular user can only retrieve data about a team if that team is part of a private league of which the user is a member, or if its in a public league.
  HTTP Operations Supported:
    - GET
  URIs:
    https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/team/
    Any sub-resource under a team is extracted using a URI like:
      https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/team//
    Multiple sub-resources can be extracted from team in the same URI using a format like:
      https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/team/;out=,{sub_resource_2}
  Team key format:
    .l.{league_id}.t.{team_id}
    Example: pnfl.l.431.t.1 or 223.l.431.t.1
  Sub-resources:
    Default sub-resource: metadata
```

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

```XML
    <action>accept</action>
```

### API Documentation for PUT /fantasy/v2/transaction/

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

This section describes the `PUT` endpoint for managing transactions in the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API. It allows editing waiver claims and managing pending trades. Only `waiver` and `pending_trade` transaction types are supported for `PUT` operations.

```APIDOC
Endpoint: PUT /fantasy/v2/transaction/
Description: Edits waiver priority or FAAB bid for pending waiver claims, or accepts/rejects/allows/disallows/votes against trades.
Supported Transaction Types: waiver, pending_trade
```

```XML
    <scoring_type>head</scoring_type>
    <current_week>16</current_week>
    <start_week>1</start_week>
    <end_week>16</end_week>
    <is_finished>1</is_finished>
    <scoreboard>

        <matchup>
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports Players Collection API Reference

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Provides comprehensive access to player information, allowing retrieval of single or multiple players, with options for filtering and extracting specific sub-resources. This API supports various qualification methods based on game, league, or team context.

```APIDOC
Players collection:
  Description: With the Players API, you can obtain information from a collection of players simultaneously. To obtains general players information, the players collection can be qualified in the URI by a particular game, league or team. To obtain specific league or team related information, the players collection is qualified by the relevant league or team. Each element beneath the Players Collection will be a Player Resource.

  HTTP Operations Supported:
    - GET

  URIs:
    Any sub-resource valid for a player is a valid sub-resource under the players collection.
    - /players/{sub_resource}
    - /players;player_keys={player_key1},{player_key2}/{sub_resource}
    - /players;out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}
    - /players;player_keys={player_key1},{player_key2};out={sub_resource_1},{sub_resource_2}

  Filters:
    The players collection can have filters such as the following to obtain a subset of a players collection that satisfy the filtering condition. The filters can be combined to obtain a more restricted list of players.
    - parameter: position
      values: Valid player positions
      usage: /players;position=QB (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: status
      values: A (all available players), FA (free agents only), W (waivers only), T (all taken players), K (keepers only)
      usage: /players;status=A (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: search
      values: player name
      usage: /players;search=smith (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: sort
      values: {stat_id}, NAME (last, first), OR (overall rank), AR (actual rank), PTS (fantasy points)
      usage: /players;sort=60 (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: sort_type
      values: season, date (baseball, basketball, and hockey only), week (football only), lastweek (baseball, basketball, and hockey only), lastmonth
      usage: /players;sort_type=season (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: sort_season
      values: year
      usage: /players;sort_type=season;sort_season=2010 (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: sort_date (baseball, basketball, and hockey only)
      values: YYYY-MM-DD
      usage: /players;sort_type=date;sort_date=2010-02-01 (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: sort_week (football only)
      values: week
      usage: /players;sort_type=week;sort_week=10 (Note: Applied only in a leagues context)
    - parameter: start
      values: Any integer 0 or greater
      usage: /players;start=25
    - parameter: count
      values: Any integer greater than 0
      usage: /players;count=5
```

--------------------------------

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: Games Collection Filters

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Describes the filter parameters available for the games collection, allowing users to obtain a subset of games that satisfy specific conditions. Filters can be combined for more restricted results.

```APIDOC
Filter parameter | Filter parameter values | Usage
-----------------|-------------------------|-------
is_available     | `1` to only show games currently in season | `/games;is_available=1`
game_types       | `full`|`pickem-team`|`pickem-group`|`pickem-team-list` | `/games;game_types=full,pickem-team`
game_codes       | Any valid game codes    | `/games;game_codes=nfl,mlb`
seasons          | Any valid seasons       | `/games;seasons=2011,2012`
```

### PHP Storing OAuth Access Token Data to File

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

This PHP snippet illustrates how to persist the obtained OAuth access token, secret, and session handle to a local file for future use, preventing repeated authentication flows. It includes basic file write operations and error handling for file access.

```php
if( $store_access_token_data ) {

  print "Looks like we need to store access token data! Doing that now.\n";

  $tok_fh = fopen( $token_file_name, 'w' );
  if( $tok_fh ) {
    fwrite( $tok_fh, "${access_token}\n" );
    fwrite( $tok_fh, "${access_secret}\n" );
    fwrite( $tok_fh, "${access_session}\n" );

    fclose( $tok_fh );
  } else {
    print "Hm, couldn't open file to write back access token information.\n";
  }
}
?>
```

### OAuth Authentication for Fantasy Sports API

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Explains that OAuth is the required authentication mechanism for the Yahoo Fantasy Sports APIs, allowing applications to make requests on behalf of users. It references Yahoo's primary OAuth documentation, specifically the Authorization Flow, and recommends using existing OAuth libraries to simplify implementation.

```APIDOC
Authentication Mechanism: OAuth
  Purpose: Allows applications to make requests on behalf of users by obtaining their permission.
  Details:
    - Based on Yahoo!'s primary OAuth documentation.
    - Key concept: OAuth Authorization Flow (explains request points and user involvement).
  Implementation Recommendation:
    - Use existing OAuth libraries (available on OAuth.net Code page) due to complexity of constructing flows from scratch.
```

### Make Signed Request to Yahoo Fantasy API (PHP)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

This function demonstrates how to make a signed request to the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API using the obtained access token and secret. It employs HMAC-SHA1 signing, which is typically required for API calls after authentication. It relies on an external `_make_signed_request` function to handle the signing and HTTP request.

```php
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//  FUNCTION make_request
/// @brief Make an actual request to the fantasy API.
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
function make_request( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $access_token, $access_token_secret, $url ) {

  $signature_method = 'hmac-sha1';

  // Make the signed request to fantasy API
  $response_data = _make_signed_request( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $access_token, $access_token_secret, $signature_method, $url );

  return $response_data;
}
```

```XML
          <is_undroppable>0</is_undroppable>

          <eligible_positions>
            <position>RP</position>
            <position>P</position>
          </eligible_positions>
          <has_player_notes>1</has_player_notes>
          <selected_position>

        </player>
```

### PHP Function for OAuth 1.0 Signed PUT/POST Requests

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

This PHP function, `make_write_request`, provides a workaround for PHP OAuth extension limitations by manually constructing and executing OAuth 1.0 signed PUT or POST requests via cURL. It's designed for interacting with APIs like Yahoo Fantasy Sports that require write operations. The function accepts consumer keys, access tokens, the HTTP method (PUT/POST), the target URL, and a file containing the data to be sent. It handles OAuth signature generation (HMAC-SHA1), parameter sorting, URL encoding, and cURL options for both POST (using `CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS`) and PUT (using `CURLOPT_INFILE` and `CURLOPT_INFILESIZE`). It also includes basic error handling for authentication failures (HTTP 401).

```PHP
<?php
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//  FUNCTION make_write_request
/// @brief Make a write (PUT/POST) request
///
/// @param[out] $auth_failure     Sets variable to true on 401 HTTP code (auth)
/// @param[in]  $consumer_key     Application consumer key
/// @param[in]  $consumer_secret  Application consumer secret
/// @param[in]  $access_token     Access token for user/application
/// @param[in]  $access_secret    Access token secret for user/application
/// @param[in]  $method           PUT or POST
/// @param[in]  $url              URL to PUT/POST against
/// @param[in]  $infile           Filename specifiying data to PUT/POST
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
function make_write_request( &$auth_failure, $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $access_token, $access_secret, $method, $url, $infile ) {

  // Make sure we can open the infile
  $in_fh = NULL;
  if( file_exists( $infile ) &&
      $in_fh = fopen( $infile, 'r' ) ) {

    $input_data = '';
    while( $line = fgets( $in_fh ) ) {
      $input_data .= $line;
    }

  } else {
    print "Cannot open infile: ${infile}\n";
    return false;
  }

  $auth_failure = false;
  $response_success = false;

  $oauth_consumer_key = $consumer_key;
  $oauth_consumer_secret = $consumer_secret;
  $oauth_token = $access_token;
  $oauth_token_secret = $access_secret;

  $oauth_signature_method = 'HMAC-SHA1';
  $oauth_nonce = rand( 0, 999999 );
  $oauth_timestamp = time();
  $oauth_version = "1.0";

  $params = array(
    'oauth_consumer_key'     => $oauth_consumer_key,
    'oauth_nonce'            => $oauth_nonce,
    'oauth_signature_method' => $oauth_signature_method,
    'oauth_timestamp'        => $oauth_timestamp,
    'oauth_token'            => $oauth_token,
    'oauth_version'          => $oauth_version,
  );

  // Params need to be sorted by key
  ksort( $params, SORT_STRING );

  // Urlencode params and generate param string
  $param_list = array();
  foreach( $params as $key => $value ) {
    $param_list[] = urlencode( $key ) . '=' . urlencode( $value );
  }
  $param_string = join( '&', $param_list );

  // Generate base string (needed for SHA1)
  $base_string = urlencode( $method ) . '&' . urlencode( $url ) . '&' .
    urlencode( $param_string );

  // Generate secret and signature
  $secret = urlencode( $consumer_secret ) . '&' . urlencode( $oauth_token_secret );
  $signature =
    base64_encode( hash_hmac( 'sha1', $base_string, $secret, true ) );

  // Append signature
  $final_url = $url . '?' . $param_string . '&oauth_signature=' . urlencode( $signature );

  // Make the curl call
  $ch = curl_init();
  curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, array( 'Content-type: application/xml' ) );
  if( $method == 'POST' ) {
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_POST, 1 );
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, $input_data );
  } else if( $method == 'PUT' ) {

    fseek( $in_fh, 0 );

    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_PUT, 1 );
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_INFILE, $in_fh );
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_INFILESIZE, strlen( $input_data ) );

  }
  curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_URL, $final_url );
  curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER, true );

  $ycw_result = curl_exec( $ch );
  $ret_code = curl_getinfo( $ch, CURLINFO_HTTP_CODE );

  fclose( $in_fh );

  curl_close( $ch );

  if( $ret_code == 401 ) {
    $auth_failure = true;
  } else {
    $response_success = true;
  }

  print "Return code: ${ret_code}\n";
  print "Response from API:\n";
  print_r( $ycw_result );

  return $response_success;
}
?>
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: Games Collection Filters

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Details the available filter parameters for the games collection, allowing users to obtain a subset of games based on criteria like availability, game types, codes, and seasons. Filters can be combined for more specific results.

```APIDOC
Filter parameter | Filter parameter values | Usage
-----------------|-------------------------|-------
is_available     | `1` to only show games currently in season | `/games;is_available=1`
game_types       | `full`|`pickem-team`|`pickem-group`|`pickem-team-list` | `/games;game_types=full,pickem-team`
game_codes       | Any valid game codes    | `/games;game_codes=nfl,mlb`
seasons          | Any valid seasons       | `/games;seasons=2011,2012`
```

### OAuth Authentication for Yahoo Fantasy Sports API

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

This section explains that OAuth is the required authentication mechanism for the Fantasy Sports APIs. It highlights that users must grant permission for requests made on their behalf and points to Yahoo's primary OAuth documentation for detailed information, specifically the OAuth Authorization Flow. It also recommends using existing OAuth libraries to simplify implementation.

```APIDOC
If youre going to use the Fantasy Sports APIs, youre going to have to get a bit familiar with OAuth. OAuth is the authentication mechanism for these services that allows users to grant you permission to make requests on their behalf. Many other Yahoo! services use OAuth, and thus all of the underlying details are explained in exhaustive detail in our primary OAuth documentation. Of particular interest is the OAuth Authorization Flow, which explains where each request is made and where the user needs to get involved.

However, constructing OAuth flows from scratch is complicated and easy to get wrong. Its often easier to use existing libraries, which are available for most languages on the OAuth.net Code page.
```

### PHP Function for OAuth 1.0a Signed PUT/POST Requests

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

The `make_write_request` PHP function facilitates sending authenticated PUT or POST requests to an OAuth 1.0a protected API. It manually constructs the OAuth signature, including consumer and access tokens, and uses cURL to execute the HTTP request. The function supports reading request body data from a specified input file and handles response codes, specifically flagging authentication failures (401).

```php
<?php
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//  FUNCTION make_write_request
/// @brief Make a write (PUT/POST) request
///
/// @param[out] $auth_failure     Sets variable to true on 401 HTTP code (auth)
/// @param[in]  $consumer_key     Application consumer key
/// @param[in]  $consumer_secret  Application consumer secret
/// @param[in]  $access_token     Access token for user/application
/// @param[in]  $access_secret    Access token secret for user/application
/// @param[in]  $method           PUT or POST
/// @param[in]  $url              URL to PUT/POST against
/// @param[in]  $infile           Filename specifiying data to PUT/POST
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
function make_write_request( &$auth_failure, $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $access_token, $access_secret, $method, $url, $infile ) {

  // Make sure we can open the infile
  $in_fh = NULL;
  if( file_exists( $infile ) &&
      $in_fh = fopen( $infile, 'r' ) ) {

    $input_data = '';
    while( $line = fgets( $in_fh ) ) {
      $input_data .= $line;
    }

  } else {
    print "Cannot open infile: ${infile}\n";
    return false;
  }

  $auth_failure = false;
  $response_success = false;

  $oauth_consumer_key = $consumer_key;
  $oauth_consumer_secret = $consumer_secret;
  $oauth_token = $access_token;
  $oauth_token_secret = $access_secret;

  $oauth_signature_method = 'HMAC-SHA1';
  $oauth_nonce = rand( 0, 999999 );
  $oauth_timestamp = time();
  $oauth_version = "1.0";

  $params = array(
    'oauth_consumer_key'     => $oauth_consumer_key,
    'oauth_nonce'            => $oauth_nonce,
    'oauth_signature_method' => $oauth_signature_method,
    'oauth_timestamp'        => $oauth_timestamp,
    'oauth_token'            => $oauth_token,
    'oauth_version'          => $oauth_version,
  );

  // Params need to be sorted by key
  ksort( $params, SORT_STRING );

  // Urlencode params and generate param string
  $param_list = array();
  foreach( $params as $key => $value ) {
    $param_list[] = urlencode( $key ) . '=' . urlencode( $value );
  }
  $param_string = join( '&', $param_list );

  // Generate base string (needed for SHA1)
  $base_string = urlencode( $method ) . '&' . urlencode( $url ) . '&' .
    urlencode( $param_string );

  // Generate secret and signature
  $secret = urlencode( $consumer_secret ) . '&' . urlencode( $oauth_token_secret );
  $signature =
    base64_encode( hash_hmac( 'sha1', $base_string, $secret, true ) );

  // Append signature
  $final_url = $url . '?' . $param_string . '&oauth_signature=' . urlencode( $signature );

  // Make the curl call
  $ch = curl_init();
  curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, array( 'Content-type: application/xml' ) );
  if( $method == 'POST' ) {
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_POST, 1 );
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, $input_data );
  } else if( $method == 'PUT' ) {

    fseek( $in_fh, 0 );

    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_PUT, 1 );
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_INFILE, $in_fh );
    curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_INFILESIZE, strlen( $input_data ) );

  }
  curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_URL, $final_url );
  curl_setopt( $ch, CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER, true );

  $ycw_result = curl_exec( $ch );
  $ret_code = curl_getinfo( $ch, CURLINFO_HTTP_CODE );

  fclose( $in_fh );

  curl_close( $ch );

  if( $ret_code == 401 ) {
    $auth_failure = true;
  } else {
    $response_success = true;
  }

  print "Return code: ${ret_code}\n";
  print "Response from API:\n";
  print_r( $ycw_result );

  return $response_success;
}
?>
```

--------------------------------

### Transactions Collection Filtering Parameters

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Details the available filter parameters for the transactions collection, allowing users to obtain a subset of transactions that satisfy specific conditions. Filters can be combined for more restricted results.

```APIDOC
Transactions Collection Filters:
  - type: add, drop, commish, trade (e.g., /transactions;type=add)
  - types: Any valid types (e.g., /transactions;types=add,trade)
  - team_key: A team_key within the league (e.g., /transactions;team_key=257.l.193.t.1)
  - type with team_key: waiver, pending_trade (requires team_key, e.g., /transactions;team_key=257.l.193.t.1;type=waiver)
  - count: Any integer greater than 0 (e.g., /transactions;count=5)
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports Team XML Structure

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Defines the XML schema for a single team object within the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API, detailing its properties such as team key, ID, name, URLs, division, FAAB balance, playoff status, manager details, season points, and standing outcomes.

```APIDOC
Team Object (XML Element: <team>)
  team_key: string
  team_id: integer
  name: string
  url: string
  team_logos: object (XML Element: <team_logos>)
    team_logo: object (XML Element: <team_logo>)
      size: string (e.g., "medium")
      url: string
  division_id: integer
  faab_balance: integer
  clinched_playoffs: integer
  managers: object (XML Element: <managers>)
    manager: object (XML Element: <manager>)
      manager_id: integer
      nickname: string
      guid: string
  team_points: object (XML Element: <team_points>)
    coverage_type: string (e.g., "season")
    season: integer
    total: float
  team_standings: object (XML Element: <team_standings>)
    rank: integer
    outcome_totals: object (XML Element: <outcome_totals>)
      wins: integer
      losses: integer
      ties: integer
      percentage: float
    divisional_outcome_totals: object (XML Element: <divisional_outcome_totals>)
      wins: integer
      losses: integer
      ties: integer
```

### Drop Player from Team via Yahoo Fantasy Sports API (XML)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

XML payload for a POST request to the transactions API to drop a player from a fantasy team. Requires the player's key and the source team's key.

```XML
<fantasy_content>
  <transaction>
    <type>drop</type>
    <player>
      <player_key>{player_key}</player_key>
      <transaction_data>
        <type>drop</type>
        <source_team_key>{team_key}</source_team_key>
      </transaction_data>
    </player>
  </transaction>
</fantasy_content>
```

### PUT Request: Reject Pending Trade

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

XML payload for rejecting a pending trade proposal. The request requires the `transaction_key` of the trade and sets the `action` to 'reject'. An optional `trade_note` can be included.

```XML
<?xml version='1.0'?>
<fantasy_content>
  <transaction>
    <transaction_key>248.l.55438.pt.11</transaction_key>
    <type>pending_trade</type>
    <action>reject</action>
    <trade_note>No way!</trade_note>
  </transaction>
</fantasy_content>
```

### PHP OAuth API Data Fetching with Stored Access Token

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

This PHP snippet shows how to use a previously obtained OAuth access token and secret to make authenticated API requests to the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API. It includes error handling for API call failures and prints the response.

```php
if( $access_token ) {

  // Try to make request using stored token
  try {
    $o->setToken( $access_token, $access_secret );
    if( $o->fetch( $url ) ) {
      print "Got data from API:\n\n";
      print $o->getLastResponse() . "\n\n";

      print "Successful!\n";
    } else {
      print "Couldn'\t fetch\n";
    }
  } catch( OAuthException $e ) {
    print 'Error: ' . $e->getMessage() . "\n";
    print 'Error Code: ' . $e->getCode() . "\n";
    print 'Response: ' . $e->lastResponse . "\n";
  }
}
```

```APIDOC
    team_key (string): Unique identifier for the fantasy team (e.g., 223.l.431.t.1).
```

### Filter Parameters for Transactions Collection

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Details the available filter parameters for the transactions collection, allowing users to obtain a subset of transactions based on criteria such as type, team key, or count. Filters can be combined for more restricted results.

```APIDOC
Filter Parameters:
| Parameter           | Values                      | Usage Example                                            |
|---------------------|-----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|
| type                | add,drop,commish,trade      | /transactions;type=add                                   |
| types               | Any valid types             | /transactions;types=add,trade                            |
| team_key            | A [team_key](#team-resource-key_format) within the league | /transactions;team_key=257.l.193.t.1                     |
| type with team_key  | waiver,pending_trade        | /transactions;team_key=257.l.193.t.1;type=waiver         |
| count               | Any integer greater than 0  | /transactions;count=5                                    |
```

### Yahoo Fantasy Sports API: PUT Transaction Resource

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Documentation for the `PUT` method on the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API transaction resource. This method allows editing waiver priority or FAAB bids for pending waiver claims, and managing trade proposals (accepting, rejecting, allowing, disallowing, voting against). It is only applicable to `waiver` or `pending_trade` transaction types.

```APIDOC
Method: PUT
Endpoint: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/transaction/
Supported Transaction Types: waiver, pending_trade

Usage:
- Edit waiver priority or FAAB bid for pending waiver claims.
- Accept or reject trade proposals.
- Allow or vote against trades (if league settings permit).
```

```APIDOC
  Parameters:
    team_key (string): Unique identifier for the fantasy team.

```

### Make Authenticated Yahoo Fantasy Sports API Request (PHP)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Performs an authenticated request to the Yahoo Fantasy Sports API using the obtained OAuth 1.0a access token and secret. This function uses the more secure 'hmac-sha1' signature method for signing the request, which is standard for API interactions.

```php
function make_request( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $access_token, $access_token_secret, $url ) {

  $signature_method = 'hmac-sha1';

  // Make the signed request to fantasy API
  $response_data = _make_signed_request( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $access_token, $access_token_secret, $signature_method, $url );

  return $response_data;
}
```

--------------------------------

### Exchange Request Token for Access Token (PHP)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

This function completes the OAuth 1.0a handshake by exchanging the authorized request token and a user-provided verifier for a long-lived access token. It also uses plaintext signing and targets Yahoo's OAuth endpoint. It depends on external `_make_signed_request` and `oauth_response_to_array` functions.

```php
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//  FUNCTION get_access_token
/// @brief Get an access token for a certain user and a certain application,
///        based on the request token and verifier
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
function get_access_token( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $request_token, $request_token_secret, $verifier ) {

  $url = 'https://api.login.yahoo.com/oauth/v2/get_token';
  $signature_method = 'plaintext';

  // Add in the oauth verifier
  $params = array( 'oauth_verifier' => $verifier );

  // Make the signed request using the request_token data
  $response_data = _make_signed_request( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $request_token, $request_token_secret, $signature_method, $url, $params );

  if( $response_data && $response_data['return_code'] == 200 ) {

    $contents = $response_data['contents'];
    $data = oauth_response_to_array( $contents );

    //print_r( $data );

    return $data;
  }

  return false;
}
```

### Exchange Request Token for Access Token (PHP)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Exchanges a previously obtained OAuth 1.0a request token and a user-provided verifier for a long-lived access token. This access token is essential for making authenticated API calls. Similar to the request token step, it uses a 'plaintext' signature method.

```php
function get_access_token( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $request_token, $request_token_secret, $verifier ) {

  $url = 'https://api.login.yahoo.com/oauth/v2/get_token';
  $signature_method = 'plaintext';

  // Add in the oauth verifier
  $params = array( 'oauth_verifier' => $verifier );

  // Make the signed request using the request_token data
  $response_data = _make_signed_request( $consumer_key, $consumer_secret, $request_token, $request_token_secret, $signature_method, $url, $params );

  if( $response_data && $response_data['return_code'] == 200 ) {

    $contents = $response_data['contents'];
    $data = oauth_response_to_array( $contents );

    //print_r( $data );

    return $data;
  }

  return false;
}
```

### Cancel Pending Waiver Claim or Trade (DELETE)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/index

Describes how to use the DELETE HTTP method to cancel pending waiver claims or proposed trades. Specifies the URL and conditions for deletion, noting that only 'waiver' or 'pending_trade' types can be deleted if the trade has not yet been accepted.

```APIDOC
DELETE https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/transaction/
  Description: Cancels any pending waiver claim or proposed trade.
  Conditions: Only 'waiver' or 'pending_trade' types can be deleted if the trade has not yet been accepted.
```

--------------------------------

### Cancel Pending Waiver Claim or Trade (DELETE)

Source: https://developer.yahoo.com/fantasysports/guide

Describes how to use the DELETE HTTP method to cancel pending waiver claims or proposed trades. This operation is restricted to specific transaction types and conditions.

```APIDOC
Method: DELETE
Endpoint: https://fantasysports.yahooapis.com/fantasy/v2/transaction/
Purpose: Cancel any pending waiver claim or proposed trade.
Conditions:
  - Only 'waiver' or 'pending_trade' types.
  - Pending trade must not yet be accepted.
```
